-\n\nPhased\n\nconfigurations\nArray\n\n(Figure\n\nE1 to\n\nE3 are\n\nelectronic\n\nscan\n\ntypes.\n\n2-13)\n\nAs described\nin detail\nin the Phase A report\nthe large\nsize\nof\nthis\narray\nis\ndriven\nby\nthe attempt\nto achieve\n54 dB of peak gain over the coverage\narea\nwith\na single\ntransmit/receive\naperture\nwith\nshared\nphase shifters.\nIf\nseparate\ntransmit\nand\nreceive\napertures\nare\nused,,\nthe\nsize\nof each aperture\ncan be\nsubstantially\nreduced.\nFor the transmit\nphased\narray,,\nthe phase shifter\n(with\na loss\nof 3 dB - see\nPhase A report)\ncan be moved to the low power side\nof the amplifier,,\nthe\nfilter\nrequirements\nwould be substantially\neased resulting\nin about\n0.2 dB loss,,\nand no\ncirculator\n(0.2\ndB loss)\nis needed.\nThis\nreduction\nof 4.0 dB of loss\nbetween\nthe\namplifier\noutput\nand\nthe\nhorn\nelement\nmeans that\na transmit\narray\nof about\n10,,000 elements\nwould be adequate\n(44" x 44").\nFor the receive\narray,,\nthe\nphase\nshifter\nmust\nstill\nbe\nbetween\nthe horn and the summing network\nto avoid\nthe\nrequirement\nfor thousands\nof mixers,,\nlow\nnoise\namplifiers,,\nand\na means\nof\ngenerating\nthousands\nof coherent\nmm LO signals\n(i.e.\ngenerating\ni0 W at 40 GHz\nand dividing\nit\n12,,600 ways with\na low loss\nwaveguide\npower divider).\nThe\nphase\nshifter\ncan\nbe\na ferrite,,\nnon-reciprocal\ndevice,,\nhowever,,\nwith\nonly\n1.0 dB of\nloss.\nThe receive\narray\ncould\nbe realized\nwith\nabout 12,,600\nhorns\n(48"\nx\n48").\nThus\nby\nusing\nseparate\ntransmit\nand receive\narrays,,\nthe total\nnumber of horns\nrequired\nwould be reduced\nby about\n15%.\nThe\nDC to\nRF efficiency\nwould\nbe\nincreased\n2.5\ntimes,,\nthe antenna\nbeamwidth\nwould\nincrease\nby 63%,, and thermal\nand mechanical\nassembly\nproblems\nwould\nbe eased.\nThe implications\nof\nmultibeam\noperation\nfrom a single\narray\nare discussed\nin Appendix\nA of the Phase A report.\nThe\n\nlist\n\nelements\nto\noverwhelming\nagility\nand\n\nof\n\nmajor\n\nweaknesses\n\nprovide\n54 dB of gain\nover\ndisadvantage\nwhich\ncannot\ninertia-free\nbeam scan.\n\nspeaks\n\nfor\n\nitself.\n\nThe\n\nlarge\n\na\nscan\nangle\nof\n+I3YOO2oZO02\nbe made up by the tw_ advantages\n\nnumber\n\nI\nII\nI\nl\nI\nl\nl\nl\nl\n\nof\n\nis\nan\nof beam\n\nOne other\nfactor\nmust be considered\nin the use of a phased array:\nThe power\nconsumed\nby the phase shifter\nand\nits\nassociated\ncircuitry.\nAt\nthe\npresent\nstate-of-the-art,,\ndiode\n5 bit\nphase shifters\nrequire\nabout\ni00 mw of continuous\npower.\nNot only must provision\nbe made to supply\nthe required\n2 to 3 kw of power\nper array\nbut the thermal\nproblem\narising\nfrom the phase shifters\nwould\nexceed\nthat\nof the amplifiers\nand would require\na large\ndedicated\nradiator\narea.\nUsing\nseparate\narrays\nfor transmit\nand POOR\n\nPAGE IS\nO_LtTY\n\nJ\n\nI\nI\nI\nI\nI\nI\nI\nI\n\nORIGINAL PAGE IS\nOF POOR QUALITY\n\nFamily\nof Reflectors\nMounted on Beam\nWaveguide\n\nGimba]\n\nAssembly\n\nThe antenna gimbal assembly is isolated from the external\n\norbital\n\nenvironment\n\nin order to minimize the temperature effects on the pointing and operational\nrequirements of the system. The external surfaces of the gimbal housing is\nwrapped with multi-layer\nthermal blankets. The heat path across the antenna/\ngimbal housing interface is isolated by the use of thermal spacers. Because\nof the close fit of the bearings, it will be necessary to add heaters on\nthe elevation axis bearing housing and/or shaft.\nThe heaters will provide\na constant temperature gradient across the bearings, thereby maintaining\nthe established operating preload. Both prime and redundant heaters will\nbe required for reliable operation and the deisgn will\nsize for a 50%duty cycle.\n3.2.4\n\nElectronics\n\n3.2.4.1\n\nEquipment\n\nhousing\n\nArrangement\n\nStructural\n\nberyllium.\n\nI0\n\nThe\n\nassembly.\nfor\n\ngimbal\n\nto the structural\n\nRF components\n\nare
